import java.util.Scanner;

/*
* To change this license header, choose License Headers in Project Properties.
* To change this template file, choose Tools | Templates
* and open the template in the editor.
*/

/**
*
* @author My PC
*/
public class Triangle {

float a, b, c;

public Triangle() {
}

public Triangle(float a, float b, float c) {
this.a = a;
this.b = b;
this.c = c;
}

public int isTriangle() {
if ((a + b) > c && (a + c) > b && (c + b) > a && a > 0 && b > 0 && c > 0) {
return 1;
} else {
return 0;
}
}

public int isEquilateral() {
if ((a == b) && (a == c)) {
return 1;
} else {
return 0;
}
}

public int isIsoceles() {
if (a == b || a == c || b == c) {
return 1;

} else {
return 0;
}
}

public int isRightIsosceles() {
if (((a * a + b * b == c * c) && (a == b)) || ((a * a + c * c == b * b) && (a == c)) || ((b * b + b * b == a * a) && (c == b))) {
return 1;
} else {
return 0;
}
}

public int isRight() {
if ((a * a == b * b + c * c) || (b * b == a * a + c * c) || (c * c == a * a + b * b)) {
return 1;
} else {
return 0;
}
}

public void getType() {
if (isEquilateral() == 1) {
System.out.println("La tam giac deu");
} else {
if (isIsoceles() == 1) {
System.out.println("La tam giac can");
} else {
if (isRightIsosceles() == 1) {
System.out.println("La tam giac vuong can");
} else {
if (isRight() == 1) {
System.out.println("La tam giac vuong");

} else {
System.out.println("Khong phai 3 canh tam giac");
}
}
}
}
}
public double Area(){
float s=(a+b+c)/2;
return (float) Math.sqrt(s*(s-a)*(s-b)*(s-c));

}
public void Display(){
if (isTriangle()==1) {
System.out.println("Ba canh tam giac la: a="+a+", b="+b+", c"+c);
getType();
System.out.println("Dien tich la: "+Area());
} else {
System.out.println("Nhap lai 3 canh");
}
}
public static void main(String[] args){
Scanner sc=new Scanner(System.in);
float a,b,c;
a=sc.nextFloat();
b=sc.nextFloat();
c=sc.nextFloat();
Triangle A=new Triangle(a, b, c);
A.Display();
}



}

#include<stdio.h>
#include<string.h>
int demtu(int dem,int i,int n,char *s){
if(i == (n - 1))
return dem;
if(i == 0 && s[i] != ' ')
dem = 1;
if(s[i] == ' ' && s[i + 1] != ' ')
dem++;
return demtu(dem,i + 1,n,s);
}
main() {
char s[100];
int kq,dem = 0;
int n,i = 0;
printf("nhap chuoi: ");
gets(s);
n = strlen(s);
kq = demtu(dem,i,n,s);
printf("\nSo tu trong chuoi la: %d",kq);
}

#include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>

int demTu(char *strHieu,int dem,int n)
{
if(n>strlen(strHieu)-3)
return dem;
if(strHieu[n]!=32 && n==0)
++dem;
if(strHieu[n]==32 && strHieu[n+1]!=32)
{
++dem;
return demTu(strHieu,dem,(n+1));
}
else
return demTu(strHieu,dem,(n+1));
}
main()
{
char strHieu[100];
printf("Nhap chuoi bat ky: ");
gets(strHieu);
printf("%d" ,demTu(strHieu,0,0));
}

#include <stdio.h>
#include <math.h>

int Ngto(int n,int i)
{
if(n<2)
return 0;
if (i>1)
if (n%i == 0)
return 0;
else
return Ngto(n,i-1);
else
return 1;
}

int Sohh(int n,int i)
{
if (i==1)
return 1;
if (n%i == 0)
return i+Sohh(n,i-1);
else
return Sohh(n,i-1);

}

main()
{
int n;
scanf("%d" ,&n);
if(Ngto(n,sqrt(n))==0)
printf("ko phai so ngto\n");
else
printf("La so ngto\n");
if(Sohh(n,n/2)==n)
printf("La so hoan thien");
else
printf("khong phai so hoan thien");
}

#include <stdio.h>

int tichchan(int n)
{
if(n==0)
return 1;
if((n%10)%2==0)
return (n%10)*tichchan(n/10);
else
return tichchan(n/10);
}
int chanle(int n)
{
if(n==0)
return 1;
if(n%2!=0)
return 0;
else
return chanle(n/10);
}
main()
{
int n;
scanf("%d" ,&n);
if(tichchan(n)==1)
if(chanle(n)==0)
printf("0");
else
printf("1");
else
printf("Tich chan la: %d" ,tichchan(n));
}

import java.util.Scanner;
public class Armstrong {

public static void main(String[] args) {
int n, num = 0, x, sum = 0, y;
Scanner count = new Scanner(System.in);
System.out.println("Nhap n: ");
n = count.nextInt();
x = n;
y = n;
while (x != 0) {
num = num + 1;
x = x / 10;
}
while (y != 0) {
sum = (int) (sum + Math.pow((y % 10), num));
y = y / 10;

}
if (sum == n) {
System.out.println("La so Armstrong");
} else {
System.out.println("Khong phai so Armstrong");
}

}
}

import java.util.Scanner;

/*
* To change this license header, choose License Headers in Project Properties.

*/
/**
*
* @author PC
*/
/*Nguyen Van Hai_1811505310213*/
public class Armstrong {

public static void main(String[] args) {
int n, num = 0, x, sum = 0, y;
Scanner count = new Scanner(System.in);
System.out.println("Nhap n: ");
n = count.nextInt();
x = n;
y = n;
while (x != 0) {
num = num + 1;
x = x / 10;
}
while (y != 0) {
sum = (int) (sum + Math.pow((y % 10), num));
y = y / 10;

}
if (sum == n) {
System.out.println("La so Armstrong");
} else {
System.out.println("Khong phai so Armstrong");
}

}
}

#include <stdio.h>
struct Node_List
{
int soMu, coSo;
Node_List *Adr_ItAf;
};

Node_List *Add_Af(Node_List *Hd, Node_List *It)
{
if(Hd==NULL)
Hd=It;
else
{
Node_List *tmp;
tmp=Hd;
while(tmp->Adr_ItAf!=NULL)
tmp=tmp->Adr_ItAf;
tmp->Adr_ItAf=It;
}
return Hd;
}

main()
{
int n;
Node_List *Hd,*It,*tmp;
Hd=NULL;
printf("Nhap so phan tu cua da thuc: ");
scanf("%d" ,&n);
for(int i=1;i<=n;++i)
{
It= new Node_List;
printf("Nhap co so cua ptu %d: " ,i);
scanf("%d" ,&It->coSo);
printf("Nhap so mu cua ptu %d:" ,i);
scanf("%d" ,&It->soMu);
printf("\n");
It->Adr_ItAf=NULL;
Hd=Add_Af(Hd,It);
}
tmp=Hd;
while(tmp!=NULL)
{
if(tmp->coSo%2==0)
printf(" %d(x)^%d + " ,tmp->coSo ,tmp->soMu);
tmp=tmp->Adr_ItAf;
}
printf("0");
}
